<h1 class="firstHeading mw-first-heading" id="firstHeading"><span class="mw-page-title-main">三角形</span></h1>
<div class="vector-body" id="bodyContent">
<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">维基百科，自由的百科全书</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div id="contentSub2"></div>
<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">跳到导航</a>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">跳到搜索</a>
<div class="mw-body-content mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="zh"><div class="mw-parser-output"><table cellspacing="3" class="infobox" <div class="floatright"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Trikotnik.png"><img alt="Trikotnik.png" data-file-height="330" data-file-width="539" decoding="async" height="184" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Trikotnik.png/300px-Trikotnik.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Trikotnik.png/450px-Trikotnik.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/bd/Trikotnik.png 2x" width="300"/></a></div>
<p><b>三角形</b>，又稱三邊形（英語： Triangle），是由三条<a href="/wiki/%E7%BA%BF%E6%AE%B5" title="线段">线段</a>顺次首尾相连，或不共線的三點兩兩連接，所组成的一个闭合的平面<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95%E5%9C%96%E5%BD%A2" title="幾何圖形">几何图形</a>，是最基本和最少邊的<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%9A%E8%BE%B9%E5%BD%A2" title="多边形">多边形</a>。
</p><p>一般用大写英语字母<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</semantics>

</p>

<h2><span id=".E5.88.86.E7.B1.BB"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="分类">分类</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：分类">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E4.BB.A5.E8.A7.92.E5.BA.A6.E5.88.86.E9.A1.9E"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="以角度分類">以角度分類</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：以角度分類">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h4><span id=".E9.94.90.E8.A7.92.E4.B8.89.E8.A7.92.E5.BD.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="锐角三角形">锐角三角形</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：锐角三角形">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>銳角三角形的所有內角均為<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%94%90%E8%A7%92" title="锐角">銳角</a>。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E9.92.9D.E8.A7.92.E4.B8.89.E8.A7.92.E5.BD.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="钝角三角形">钝角三角形</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：钝角三角形">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>鈍角三角形是其中一角為<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%92%9D%E8%A7%92" title="钝角">鈍角</a>的三角形，其余兩角均小於90°。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E7.9B.B4.E8.A7.92.E4.B8.89.E8.A7.92.E5.BD.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="直角三角形">直角三角形</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：直角三角形">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="floatright"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Right_triangle.png"><img alt="Right triangle.png" data-file-height="129" data-file-width="268" decoding="async" height="129" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/6/69/Right_triangle.png" width="268"/></a></div>
<p>有一个角是<a href="/wiki/%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92" title="直角">直角</a>（90°）的三角形为<a href="/wiki/%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2" title="直角三角形">直角三角形</a>。成直角的两条边称为「<a href="/wiki/%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E9%82%8A" title="直角邊">直角邊</a>」（cathetus），直角所对的边是「<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%9C%E9%82%8A" title="斜邊">斜邊</a>」（hypotenuse）；或最長的邊稱為「弦」，底部的一邊稱作「勾」（又作「句」），另一邊稱為「股」。斜邊乘上斜邊上的高÷2=勾股相乘÷2=此直角三角形面積（ch=ab）
</p>
<h4><span id=".E4.B8.89.E8.A7.92.E5.87.BD.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="三角函数">三角函数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：三角函数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="三角函数">三角函数</a></div>
<p>直角三角形各邊與角度的關係，可以三角比表示。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E4.BB.A5.E9.82.8A.E9.95.B7.E5.88.86.E9.A1.9E"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="以邊長分類">以邊長分類</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：以邊長分類">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table style="margin:auto; text-align:center">
<tbody><tr>
<td><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Triangle.Scalene.svg" title="不等邊三角形"><img alt="不等邊三角形" data-file-height="110" data-file-width="245" decoding="async" height="110" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/Triangle.Scalene.svg/245px-Triangle.Scalene.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/Triangle.Scalene.svg/368px-Triangle.Scalene.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/Triangle.Scalene.svg/490px-Triangle.Scalene.svg.png 2x" width="245"/></a>

<h4><span id=".E4.B8.8D.E7.AD.89.E9.82.8A.E4.B8.89.E8.A7.92.E5.BD.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="不等邊三角形">不等邊三角形</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：不等邊三角形">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>三條邊邊長皆不相等的三角形稱為<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%8D%E7%AD%89%E9%82%8A%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2" title="不等邊三角形">不等邊三角形</a>。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E7.AD.89.E9.82.8A.E4.B8.89.E8.A7.92.E5.BD.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="等邊三角形">等邊三角形</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：等邊三角形">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%AD%89%E8%BE%B9%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2" title="等边三角形">等邊三角形</a>（又称正三角形），为三边相等的三角形。其三個內角相等，均為60°。它是銳角三角形的一種。设其边长是 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> ，则其面積公式為 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {a^{2}{\sqrt {3}}}{4}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mrow>
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<msqrt>
<mn>3</mn>
</msqrt>
</mrow>
</mrow>
<mn>4</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {a^{2}{\sqrt {3}}}{4}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\frac {a^{2}{\sqrt {3}}}{4}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1f9ad3fc39486d5538f4a649aa19a916c02ef636" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:6.219ex; height:5.843ex;"/></span> 。
</p><p>等邊三角形是<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E5%9B%9B%E9%9D%A2%E9%AB%94" title="正四面體">正四面體</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E5%85%AB%E9%9D%A2%E9%AB%94" title="正八面體">正八面體</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E9%9D%A2%E9%AB%94" title="正二十面體">正二十面體</a>這三個<a href="/wiki/%E6%9F%8F%E6%8B%89%E5%9C%96%E7%AB%8B%E9%AB%94" title="柏拉圖立體">正多面體</a>面的形狀。六個边长相同的等邊三角形可以拼成一個<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E5%85%AD%E9%82%8A%E5%BD%A2" title="正六邊形">正六邊形</a>。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E7.AD.89.E8.85.B0.E4.B8.89.E8.A7.92.E5.BD.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="等腰三角形">等腰三角形</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：等腰三角形">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%AA%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E8%BE%B9%E4%B8%BA6.5%E7%9A%84%E7%AD%89%E8%85%B0%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="729" data-file-width="628" decoding="async" height="255" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%AA%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E8%BE%B9%E4%B8%BA6.5%E7%9A%84%E7%AD%89%E8%85%B0%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2.svg/220px-%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%AA%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E8%BE%B9%E4%B8%BA6.5%E7%9A%84%E7%AD%89%E8%85%B0%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%AA%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E8%BE%B9%E4%B8%BA6.5%E7%9A%84%E7%AD%89%E8%85%B0%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2.svg/330px-%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%AA%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E8%BE%B9%E4%B8%BA6.5%E7%9A%84%E7%AD%89%E8%85%B0%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%AA%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E8%BE%B9%E4%B8%BA6.5%E7%9A%84%E7%AD%89%E8%85%B0%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2.svg/440px-%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%AA%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E8%BE%B9%E4%B8%BA6.5%E7%9A%84%E7%AD%89%E8%85%B0%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%AA%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E8%BE%B9%E4%B8%BA6.5%E7%9A%84%E7%AD%89%E8%85%B0%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2.svg" title="放大"></a></div>等腰直角三角形只有一種形狀，其中兩个角為45度。</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E7%AD%89%E8%85%B0%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2" title="等腰三角形">等腰三角形</a>是三条<a href="/wiki/%E9%82%8A_(%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95)" title="邊 (幾何)">边</a>中有两条边相等（或是其中兩隻內角相等）的三角形。等腰三角形中的两条相等的边被称为「腰」，而另一条边被称为「底边」，两条腰交叉组成的那个点被称为「顶点」，它们组成的角被称为「顶角」。
</p><p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%AD%89%E8%BE%B9%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2" title="等边三角形">等边三角形</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%AD%89%E8%85%B0%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2" title="等腰直角三角形">等腰直角三角形</a>是等腰三角形的特殊形式。
</p><p>令其底边是 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>

等腰三角形的对应高，角平分线和中线重合。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E9.80.80.E5.8C.96.E4.B8.89.E8.A7.92.E5.BD.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="退化三角形">退化三角形</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：退化三角形">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>退化三角形是指面積為零的三角形。满足下列条件之一的三角形即可称为退化三角形：三个内角的度数为(180°,0°,0°)或(90°,90°,0°)；三边其中一条边的长度为0；一条边的长度等于另外两条之和。有人认为退化三角形并不能算是三角形，這是由於它介乎於<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E4%B8%8D%E7%AD%89%E5%BC%8F" title="三角不等式">三角不等式</a>之間，在一些資料中已否定了其中一條邊等於其餘兩條邊之和的情況。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.8B.92.E6.B4.9B.E4.B8.89.E8.A7.92.E5.BD.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="勒洛三角形">勒洛三角形</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="编辑章节：勒洛三角形">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E5%8B%92%E6%B4%9B%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2" title="勒洛三角形">勒洛三角形</a>（英語：<span lang="en">Reuleaux triangle</span>），也譯作萊洛三角形或弧三角形，又被稱為劃粉形或曲邊三角形，是除了圓形以外，最簡單易懂的勒洛多邊形，一個定寬曲線。將一個曲線圖放在兩條平行線中間，使之與這兩平行線相切，則可以做到：無論這個曲線圖如何運動，只要它還是在這兩條平行線內，就始終與這兩條平行線相切。這個定義由十九世紀的德國工程師<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Franz Reuleaux" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="弗朗茨·勒洛"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%BC%97%E6%9C%97%E8%8C%A8%C2%B7%E5%8B%92%E6%B4%9B&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="弗朗茨·勒洛（页面不存在）">弗朗茨·勒洛</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Franz_Reuleaux" title="en:Franz Reuleaux"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Franz Reuleaux</span></a></span>）</span></span>命名。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E4.B8.80.E8.88.AC.E6.80.A7.E8.B4.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="一般性质">一般性质</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="编辑章节：一般性质">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E4.B8.89.E8.A7.92.E4.B8.8D.E7.AD.89.E5.BC.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="三角不等式">三角不等式</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="编辑章节：三角不等式">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>三角边長不等式
<dl><dd>三角形两边之和大于第三边，两边之差的<a href="/wiki/%E7%BB%9D%E5%AF%B9%E5%80%BC" title="绝对值">绝对值</a>小于第三边。如果兩者相等，则是退化三角形。</dd></dl></li>
<li>三角<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%A7%E8%A7%92%E5%92%8C%E5%A4%96%E8%A7%92" title="內角和外角">內外角</a>不等式
<dl><dd>三角形任意一个外角大于不相邻的一个内角。</dd></dl></li></ul>
<h3><span id=".E8.A7.92.E5.BA.A6"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="角度">角度</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="编辑章节：角度">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="floatright"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%86%85%E8%A7%92%E3%81%A8%E5%A4%96%E8%A7%92.png"><img alt="三角形の内角と外角.png" data-file-height="143" data-file-width="190" decoding="async" height="143" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/0/0e/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%86%85%E8%A7%92%E3%81%A8%E5%A4%96%E8%A7%92.png" width="190"/></a></div>
<ul><li>三角形外角
<dl><dd>三角形兩內角之和，等於第三角的外角。</dd></dl></li>
<li>三角形內角和
<dl><dd>在歐幾里德<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E9%9D%A2_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="平面 (数学)">平面</a>內，三角形的內角和等於180°。</dd></dl></li></ul>
<h3><span id=".E5.8B.BE.E8.82.A1.E5.AE.9A.E7.90.86"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="勾股定理">勾股定理</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="编辑章节：勾股定理">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%8B%BE%E8%82%A1%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="勾股定理">勾股定理</a></div>
<p>勾股定理，又稱<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%95%A2%E6%B0%8F%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="畢氏定理">畢氏定理</a>或<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AF%95%E8%BE%BE%E5%93%A5%E6%8B%89%E6%96%AF%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="毕达哥拉斯定理">毕达哥拉斯定理</a>。其斷言，若直角三角形的其中一邊 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle c}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mrow>

</semantics>

</p>

<h3><span id=".E6.AD.A3.E5.BC.A6.E5.AE.9A.E7.90.86"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="正弦定理">正弦定理</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="编辑章节：正弦定理">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span id=".E5.85.A8.E7.AD.89.E5.8F.8A.E7.9B.B8.E4.BC.BC"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="全等及相似">全等及相似</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="编辑章节：全等及相似">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E5.85.A8.E7.AD.89.E4.B8.89.E8.A7.92.E5.BD.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="全等三角形">全等三角形</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="编辑章节：全等三角形">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%A8%E7%AD%89%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2" title="全等三角形">全等三角形</a></div>
<p>三角形具有穩定性，若二個三角形有以下的邊角關係確定後，它的形狀、大小就不會改變，二個三角形即為<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%A8%E7%AD%89%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2" title="全等三角形">全等三角形</a>。全等三角形的判斷準則有以下幾種：
</p>
<ul><li>SSS（Side-Side-Side，邊、邊、邊）：各三角形的三條邊的長度都對應地相等。</li>
<li>SAS（Side-Angle-Side，邊、角、邊）：各三角形的其中兩條邊的長度都對應地相等，且兩條邊夾著的角都對應地相等。</li>
<li>ASA（Angle-Side-Angle，角、邊、角）：各三角形的其中兩個角都對應地相等，且兩個角夾著的邊都對應地相等。</li>
<li>RHS（Right Angle-Hypotenuse-Side，直角、斜邊、邊）：在直角三角形中，斜邊及另外一條直角邊對應地相等。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li>AAS（Angle-Angle-Side，角、角、邊）：各三角形的其中兩個角都對應地相等，且其中一組對應角的對邊也對應地相等。</li></ul>
<p>SSA（Side-Side-Angle、邊、邊、角）不能保证两个三角形全等，除非該角大於等於90°，此時可以保證全等。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:34</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.9B.B8.E4.BC.BC.E4.B8.89.E8.A7.92.E5.BD.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="相似三角形">相似三角形</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="编辑章节：相似三角形">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>AA（Angle-Angle，角、角）：各三角形的其中兩個角的都對應地相等。（或稱AAA（Angle-Angle-Angle，角、角、角））</li>
<li>三邊成比例（3 sides proportional）：各三角形的三條邊的長度都成同一比例。</li>
<li>兩邊成比例且夾角相等（ratio of 2 sides, inc.∠）：各三角形的兩條邊之長度都成同一比例，且兩條邊之夾角都對應地相等。</li></ul>
<h2><span id=".E7.89.B9.E6.AE.8A.E7.B7.9A.E6.AE.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="特殊線段">特殊線段</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="编辑章节：特殊線段">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>三角形中有著一些特殊線段，是三角形研究的重要對象。
</p>
<ul><li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E7%B7%9A_(%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95%E5%AD%B8)" title="中線 (幾何學)">中線</a>(median)：三角形一边中点与这边所对頂点的连线段。</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E7%BA%BF" title="高线">高线</a>(altitude)：从三角形一个顶点向它的对边所作的垂线段。</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A7%92%E5%B9%B3%E5%88%86%E7%BA%BF" title="角平分线">角平分线</a>(angle bisector)：平分三角形一角、一个端点在这一角的对边上的线段。</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%9E%82%E7%9B%B4%E5%B9%B3%E5%88%86%E7%B7%9A" title="垂直平分線">垂直平分線</a>(perpendicular bisector)：通過三角形一边中点与該边所垂直的线段，又稱中垂线。</li></ul>
<p>以上特殊線段，每個三角形均有三條，且三線共點。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E4.B8.AD.E7.BA.BF.E9.95.BF.E5.BA.A6"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="中线长度">中线长度</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="编辑章节：中线长度">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>设在<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \Delta ABC\,}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi mathvariant="normal">Δ<!-- Δ --></mi>
<mi>A</mi>
<mi>B</mi>
<mi>C</mi>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \Delta ABC\,}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \Delta ABC\,}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f96ebbf7a74b27940dda4dc7adaa7f84275d78d0" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:7.596ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>中，若三边<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

<h3><span id=".E9.AB.98.E7.BA.BF.E9.95.BF.E5.BA.A6"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="高线长度">高线长度</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="编辑章节：高线长度">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>设在<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \Delta ABC\,}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</math></span><img alt="h_{c}={\frac {2{\sqrt {s(s-a)(s-b)(s-c)}}}{c}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6a090c145dc075d7a2c3e4729ea3a5e6bbb53e6a" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:31.249ex; height:6.176ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>其中 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle s={\frac {a+b+c}{2}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mo>=</mo>

<mi>c</mi>
</mrow>
<mn>2</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="s={\frac {a+b+c}{2}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/787a98dac5681f383514fc1bd5b4d8e561a3fd21" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:13.94ex; height:5.343ex;"/></span> 。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.A7.92.E5.B9.B3.E5.88.86.E7.BA.BF.E9.95.BF.E5.BA.A6"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="角平分线长度">角平分线长度</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="编辑章节：角平分线长度">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span id=".E4.B8.89.E8.A7.92.E5.BD.A2.E7.9A.84.E5.BF.83"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="三角形的心">三角形的心</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="编辑章节：三角形的心">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>三角形的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%85%A7%E5%BF%83" title="內心">內心</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%96%E5%BF%83" title="外心">外心</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9E%82%E5%BF%83" title="垂心">垂心</a>及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BD%A2%E5%BF%83" title="形心">形心</a>稱為三角形的四心，定義如下：
</p>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th>名称</th>
<th>定义</th>
<th>图示</th>
<th>备注
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%85%A7%E5%BF%83" title="內心">內心</a></b></td>
<td>三个內角的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A7%92%E5%B9%B3%E5%88%86%E7%BA%BF" title="角平分线">角平分线</a>的交點</td>
<td><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%86%85%E5%BF%83.png"><img alt="三角形の内心.png" data-file-height="175" data-file-width="329" decoding="async" height="133" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%86%85%E5%BF%83.png/250px-%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%86%85%E5%BF%83.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/5/59/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%86%85%E5%BF%83.png 1.5x" width="250"/></a></td>
<td>該點為三角形<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%85%A7%E5%88%87%E5%9C%93" title="內切圓">內切圓</a>的圓心。
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%96%E5%BF%83" title="外心">外心</a></b></td>
<td>三條邊的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E5%9E%82%E7%B7%9A" title="中垂線">中垂線</a>的交點</td>
<td><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%A4%96%E5%BF%83.png"><img alt="三角形の外心.png" data-file-height="263" data-file-width="266" decoding="async" height="247" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%A4%96%E5%BF%83.png/250px-%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%A4%96%E5%BF%83.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/a/a1/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%A4%96%E5%BF%83.png 1.5x" width="250"/></a></td>
<td>該點為三角形<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%96%E6%8E%A5%E5%9C%93" title="外接圓">外接圓</a>的圓心。
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9E%82%E5%BF%83" title="垂心">垂心</a></b></td>
<td>三条<a href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E7%BA%BF" title="高线">高线</a>的交點</td>
<td><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%9E%82%E5%BF%83.png"><img alt="三角形の垂心.png" data-file-height="170" data-file-width="240" decoding="async" height="177" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/7/7d/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%9E%82%E5%BF%83.png" width="250"/></a></td>
<td>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BD%A2%E5%BF%83" title="形心">形心</a>（重心）</b></td>
<td>三条<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E7%BA%BF" title="中线">中线</a>的交點</td>
<td><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E9%87%8D%E5%BF%83.png"><img alt="三角形の重心.png" data-file-height="169" data-file-width="307" decoding="async" height="138" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E9%87%8D%E5%BF%83.png/250px-%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E9%87%8D%E5%BF%83.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/8/81/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E9%87%8D%E5%BF%83.png 1.5x" width="250"/></a></td>
<td>被交点划分的线段比例为1:2（靠近角的一段较长）。
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>关于三角形的四心，有这样的一首诗：
</p>
<table class="cquote pullquote" role="presentation" style="margin:auto; display:table; border-collapse: collapse; border: none; background-color: transparent; width: auto;">
<tbody><tr>
<td style="width: 20px; vertical-align: top; border: none; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 40px; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-weight: bold; line-height: .6em; text-align: left; padding: 10px; text-orientation: upright">“
</td>
<td style="vertical-align: top; border: none; padding: 4px 10px;">內心全靠角平分，<br/>
<p>外心中點垂線伸，<br/>
垂心垂直畫三高，<br/>
形心角連線中心。
</p>
</td>
<td style="width: 20px; vertical-align: bottom; border: none; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 40px; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-weight: bold; line-height: .6em; text-align: right; padding: 10px; text-orientation: upright">”
</td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<div class="floatright"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Triangle.EulerLine.svg"><img alt="Triangle.EulerLine.svg" data-file-height="420" data-file-width="520" decoding="async" height="242" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Triangle.EulerLine.svg/300px-Triangle.EulerLine.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Triangle.EulerLine.svg/450px-Triangle.EulerLine.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Triangle.EulerLine.svg/600px-Triangle.EulerLine.svg.png 2x" width="300"/></a></div>
<p><br/>
</p><p><br/>
</p><p><br/>
</p><p><br/>
</p><p><br/>
</p><p><br/>
</p><p>垂心（蓝）、形心（黄）和外心（绿）能連成一線，且成比例1:2，稱為<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%90%E6%8B%89%E7%B7%9A" title="歐拉線">歐拉線</a>，與<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B9%9D%E9%BB%9E%E5%9C%93" title="九點圓">九點圓</a>的圓心（紅）四點共線，為垂心和形心線段的中點。
</p><p>連同以下的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%97%81%E5%BF%83" title="旁心">旁心</a>，合稱為三角形的五心：
</p>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th>名称</th>
<th>定义</th>
<th>图示</th>
<th>备注
</th></tr>
<tr>

<td>外角的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A7%92%E5%B9%B3%E5%88%86%E7%BA%BF" title="角平分线">角平分线</a>的交點</td>

<h2><span id=".E5.A4.96.E6.8E.A5.E5.9C.86.E5.92.8C.E5.86.85.E5.88.87.E5.9C.86.E5.8D.8A.E5.BE.84"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="外接圆和内切圆半径">外接圆和内切圆半径</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="编辑章节：外接圆和内切圆半径">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span id=".E9.9D.A2.E7.A9.8D"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="面積">面積</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="编辑章节：面積">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E5.9F.BA.E6.9C.AC.E5.85.AC.E5.BC.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="基本公式">基本公式</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="编辑章节：基本公式">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>三角形的面積 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 是底邊 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 與高 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle h}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>h</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle h}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="h" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b26be3e694314bc90c3215047e4a2010c6ee184a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.339ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 乘積的一半，即：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A={\frac {1}{2}}bh}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>1</mn>
<mn>2</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
<mi>b</mi>
<mi>h</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A={\frac {1}{2}}bh}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A={\frac {1}{2}}bh" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/78bb1af1b9493a6b26955f711ae9b95a68f671be" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:9.177ex; height:5.176ex;"/></span>，</dd></dl>
<p>其中的高是指底邊與對角的垂直距離。
</p>
<div class="NavFrame collapsed" style=""><div class="NavHead" style="">證明</div><div class="NavContent" style="">
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:352px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Triangle.GeometryArea.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="126" data-file-width="504" decoding="async" height="88" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Triangle.GeometryArea.svg/350px-Triangle.GeometryArea.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Triangle.GeometryArea.svg/525px-Triangle.GeometryArea.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Triangle.GeometryArea.svg/700px-Triangle.GeometryArea.svg.png 2x" width="350"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Triangle.GeometryArea.svg" title="放大"></a></div>三角形的面積可表示為一長方形面積的一半。</div></div></div>
<p>從右圖可知，將兩個全等三角形相拼，可得一平行四邊形。而將該平行四邊形分割填補，正好能得到一個面積等於 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle bh}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
<mi>h</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle bh}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle bh}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/81177b752974809f1d286901993af2f0850cbb27" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.337ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 的長方形。因此原來的三角形面積為
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A={\frac {1}{2}}bh}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>1</mn>
<mn>2</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
<mi>b</mi>
<mi>h</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A={\frac {1}{2}}bh}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A={\frac {1}{2}}bh" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/78bb1af1b9493a6b26955f711ae9b95a68f671be" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:9.177ex; height:5.176ex;"/></span>。</dd></dl>
<p>證畢。
</p>
</div></div>
<h3><span id=".E5.B7.B2.E7.9F.A5.E5.85.A9.E9.82.8A.E5.8F.8A.E5.85.B6.E5.A4.BE.E8.A7.92"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="已知兩邊及其夾角">已知兩邊及其夾角</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="编辑章节：已知兩邊及其夾角">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>設 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 為已知的兩邊， <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \gamma }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \gamma }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\gamma " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a223c880b0ce3da8f64ee33c4f0010beee400b1a" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:1.262ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 為該兩邊的夾角，則三角形面積是：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A={\frac {1}{2}}ab\sin {\gamma }}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<div class="NavFrame collapsed" style=""><div class="NavHead" style="">證明</div><div class="NavContent" style="">

<p>觀察右圖，根據<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E5%BC%A6" title="正弦">正弦</a>的定義：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sin \gamma ={\frac {h}{a}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \beta }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mtd>
</mtr>
</mtable>
</mrow>
</mstyle>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\begin{aligned}A&amp;={\frac {a^{2}\sin \beta \sin \gamma }{2\sin[180^{\circ }-(\beta +\gamma )]}}\\&amp;={\frac {a^{2}\sin \beta \sin \gamma }{2\sin(\beta +\gamma )}}\\\end{aligned}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/5b89d1a8b04836b7ba80972fe0f1b3aedb7280e5" style="vertical-align: -6.005ex; width:26.754ex; height:13.176ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>證畢。

<h3><span id=".E5.B7.B2.E7.9F.A5.E4.B8.89.E9.82.8A.E9.95.B7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="已知三邊長">已知三邊長</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="编辑章节：已知三邊長">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B5%B7%E9%BE%8D%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="海龍公式">海龍公式</a>，其表示形式為：

<div class="NavFrame collapsed" style=""><div class="NavHead" style="">證明</div><div class="NavContent" style="">
<p>无论三角形的顶点位置如何，该三角形总可以用一个直角梯形（或矩形）和两个直角三角形面积的和差来表示，而在直角坐标系中，已知直角梯形（或矩形）和直角三角形的顶点的坐标，该三角形的面积容易求出，即用上述的行列式表示。
</p>
</div></div>
<p>若三個<a href="/wiki/%E9%A0%82%E9%BB%9E_(%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95)" title="頂點 (幾何)">頂點</a>設在三維座標系上，即由 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (x_{1},y_{1},z_{1})}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<msub>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>,</mo>
<msub>
<mi>y</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>,</mo>
<msub>

<div class="NavFrame collapsed" style=""><div class="NavHead" style="">證明</div><div class="NavContent" style="">
<p><b>內切圓半徑公式</b>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%86%85%E5%BF%83.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="175" data-file-width="329" decoding="async" height="160" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%86%85%E5%BF%83.png/300px-%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%86%85%E5%BF%83.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/5/59/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%86%85%E5%BF%83.png 1.5x" width="300"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2%E3%81%AE%E5%86%85%E5%BF%83.png" title="放大"></a></div>三角形被三條角平分線分成三分。</div></div></div>
<p>根據右圖，設 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\overline {AB}}=c}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3><span id=".E5.B7.B2.E7.9F.A5.E5.85.A9.E9.82.8A.E5.90.91.E9.87.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="已知兩邊向量">已知兩邊向量</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="编辑章节：已知兩邊向量">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>設從一角出發，引出兩邊的向量為 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbf {a} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathbf {a} " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1a957216653a9ee0d0133dcefd13fb75e36b8b9d" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.299ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> 及 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbf {b} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>

<h2><span id=".E5.8D.8A.E8.A7.92.E5.AE.9A.E7.90.86"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="半角定理">半角定理</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="编辑章节：半角定理">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>在三角形<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle ABC\,}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mi>B</mi>
<mi>C</mi>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle ABC\,}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="ABC\," aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/abf5de2982b8bee6324edbbdfb50699520beefa5" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.661ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>中，三个角的半角的正切和三边有如下关系：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\begin{aligned}\tan {\frac {A}{2}}&amp;={\sqrt {\dfrac {(a+c-b)(a+b-c)}{(a+b+c)(b+c-a)}}}\\\tan {\frac {B}{2}}&amp;={\sqrt {\dfrac {(a+b-c)(b+c-a)}{(a+b+c)(a+c-b)}}}\\\tan {\frac {C}{2}}&amp;={\sqrt {\dfrac {(b+c-a)(a+c-b)}{(a+b+c)(a+b-c)}}}\\\end{aligned}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mtable columnalign="right left right left right left right left right left right left" columnspacing="0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em" displaystyle="true" rowspacing="3pt">
<mtr>
<mtd>
<mi>tan</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mi>A</mi>
<mn>2</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mtd>
<mtd>
<mi></mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<msqrt>
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mfrac>
<mrow>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
